        <meta property="og:url" content="https://pubs.acs.org/doi/full/10.1021/acsnano.3c02323"><meta property="og:title" content="High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries"><meta property="og:image" content="https://pubs.acs.org/cms/10.1021/acsnano.3c02323/asset/images/acsnano.3c02323.social.jpeg_v03"><meta property="og:description" content="Prussian blue analogues (PBAs) used as sodium ion battery (SIB) cathodes are usually the focus of attention due to their three-dimensional open frame and high theoretical capacity. Nonetheless, the disadvantages of a low working voltage and inferior structural stability of PBAs prevent their further applications. Herein, we propose constructing the Kx(MnFeCoNiCu)[Fe(CN)6] (HE-K-PBA) cathode by high-entropy and potassium incorporation strategy to simultaneously realize high working voltage and cycling stability. The reaction mechanism of metal cations in HE-K-PBA are revealed by synchrotron radiation X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS), ex situ X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (XPS), and in situ Raman spectra. We also investigate the entropy stabilization mechanism via  finite element simulation, demonstrating that HE-K-PBA with small von Mises stress and weak structure strain can significantly mitigate the structural distortion. Benefit from the stable structure and everlasting K+ (de)intercalation, the HE-K-PBA delivers high output voltage (3.46 V), good reversible capacity (120.5 mAh g–1 at 0.01 A g–1), and capacity retention of 90.4% after 1700 cycles at 1.0 A g–1. Moreover, the assembled full cell and all-solid-state batteries with a stable median voltage of 3.29 V over 3000 cycles further demonstrate the application prospects of the HE-K-PBA cathode."><meta property="og:type" content="Article"><meta property="og:site_name" content="ACS Publications"><meta name="twitter:card" content="summary_large_image"><meta name="twitter:site" content="@ACSPublications"><meta name="twitter:image" content="https://pubs.acs.org/cms/10.1021/acsnano.3c02323/asset/images/acsnano.3c02323.social.jpeg_v03">

<!-- loading Javascript for using the persistence Service -->
    <script src="/wro/1122814~thiss-ds.js" async="" nonce="93188ca2bdc0075e-SJC"></script>

    <script type="text/javascript" nonce="93188ca2bdc0075e-SJC">

        var SeamlessAccessService = {
            spUrl: "/action/ssostart",
            returnURL: window.location.href,
            my_context: 'seamlessaccess.org',
            timeout: 5000,

            getWAYFLessUrl: function (entityId) {
                return this.spUrl + "?idp=" + encodeURIComponent(entityId)
                    + "&redirectUri=" + encodeURIComponent(this.returnURL);
            },
            retrieveEntity: function (ms) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService = new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                if (ms == undefined || ms === '') {
                    ms = this.timeout;
                }

                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    persistService.entities(self.my_context)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            return resolve(res.data);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            reject('failed to retrieve entity from local storage: ' + err);
                        });
                    // Set up the timeout
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        reject('Promise timed out ' + ms + ' ms');
                    }, ms);
                });
            },
            updateEntity: function (entitydata) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService = new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                var jsonObj = {};
                try {
                    //try to parse it, if it is a json string
                    jsonObj = JSON.parse(entitydata.val());
                } catch (e) {
                    jsonObj = entitydata;
                }
                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    persistService.update(self.my_context, jsonObj)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            // Process the results
                            var ssoInstitutions = res.data;
                            return resolve(ssoInstitutions);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            console.log('failed to update the local storage due to: ' + err);
                            reject(err);
                        });
                })
            },
            removeEntity: function (entityId) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService = new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                return new Promise(function (resolve) {
                    persistService.remove(self.my_context, entityId)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            return resolve(res);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            console.log('failed to remove from local storage duo to: ' + err);
                        });
                })
            },
            getAccessibleEntityStatus: function (doi, entityId, entityTitle) {
                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: 'POST',
                        url: '/action/seamlessAccess',
                        accept: {
                            text: "application/json"
                        },
                        data: {
                            doi: doi,
                            entityid: entityId,
                            entityTitle: entityTitle,
                            eventGroupKey: '4411acd8-1824-4b0a-bcec-f960532ace9c'
                        }

                    }).done(function (status) {
                        return resolve(status);
                    }).fail(function (status) {
                        return reject(status);
                    });
                });
            },
            getEntitiesWithAllInfo: function (doi) {
                let self = this,
                    arrayOfPromises = [];
                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    self.retrieveEntity().then(function (res) {
                        let allSsoInstitutions = res;
                        for (i = 0; i < allSsoInstitutions.length; i++) {
                            let ssoInstitution = allSsoInstitutions[i];
                            arrayOfPromises.push(new Promise(function (resolve) {
                                self.getAccessibleEntityStatus(doi, ssoInstitution.entity.entityID, ssoInstitution.entity.title)
                                    .then(function (entityStatus) {
                                        resolve({
                                            entityID: ssoInstitution.entity.entityID,
                                            entityTitle: ssoInstitution.entity.title,
                                            entityStatusObj: entityStatus,
                                            entitySsoUrl: self.getWAYFLessUrl(ssoInstitution.entity.entityID)
                                        });
                                    }, function (err) {
                                        console.log('failed to get the entity status: ' + ssoInstitution.entity.entityID,err);
                                    });
                            }));
                        }
                        if(allSsoInstitutions.length === 0 && true){
                            self.getAccessibleEntityStatus(doi, null, null)
                                .then(function () {
                                    console.log('No Entity found');
                                }, function (err) {
                                    console.log('failed to get the none entity status' ,err);
                                });
                        }
                        Promise.all(arrayOfPromises)
                            .then(function (finalResponse) {
                                resolve(finalResponse);
                            }).catch(function (err) {
                                reject(err);
                            });

                    }).catch(function (err) {
                        reject(err);
                    })
                });
            }
        };

        window.addEventListener('load', function () {
            document.querySelectorAll(".sso-institution").forEach(function (institution) {
                var entityId = institution.getAttribute('data-entityid');
                var entityName = institution.getAttribute('data-name');
                var entitydata = {
                    entityID: entityId,
                    title: entityName
                };
                institution.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();

                    if ($('.institution-preference-userconsent-checkbox').length > 0) {
                        let institutionPreferenceUserConsentCheckbox = $('.institution-preference-userconsent-checkbox').get(0);
                        if (!$(institutionPreferenceUserConsentCheckbox).is(":checked")) {
                            return;
                        }
                    }

                    var self = this;
                    SeamlessAccessService.updateEntity(entitydata).then(function (res) {
                        console.log(res);
                        window.location.href = self.href;
                    }).catch(function (err) {
                        window.location.href = self.href;
                    });
                });
            });
        });

    </script>

img{border:0}.a2a_button_facebook_like iframe{max-width:none}</style><script charset="utf-8" src="https://pubs.acs.org/products/achs/releasedAssets/js/article-dc83549a302b9ecf025f.js"></script><script charset="utf-8" async="" src="https://script.hotjar.com/modules.f98993dba31a932bc912.js"></script><script id="yui__dyn_0" type="text/javascript" src="https://www2.snapengage.com/chatjs/ServiceGetConfig?w=921a4ec7-cecf-43a6-afa5-6cd1346520b1"></script><script charset="utf-8" src="https://pubs.acs.org/products/achs/releasedAssets/js/requestidlecallback-polyfill-f5170b9de43ccc25622c.js"></script><script charset="utf-8" src="https://pubs.acs.org/products/achs/releasedAssets/js/vendors~lazy-imports-c0b82d66d33565b4cebe.js"></script><script charset="utf-8" src="https://pubs.acs.org/products/achs/releasedAssets/js/lazy-imports-6922fe6a4ca6b2e0cd9a.js"></script><script type="text/javascript" src="/specs/products/achs/releasedAssets/public/mathjax-0a9852ad89643b94fe5099b753f6a294/MathJax.js?config=TeX-AMS-MML_HTMLorMML"></script><script type="text/x-mathjax-config;executed=true">MathJax.Hub.Config({
            menuSettings: {
                zoom: "Click",
                zscale: "150%"
            },
            SVG: {
                fonts: ["STIX-Web"],
                linebreaks: { automatic: true },
            },
            "HTML-CSS": {
                fonts: ["STIX"],
                linebreaks: { automatic: true },
                scale: 90,
            },
        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("mml Jax Ready", function () {
            var MML = MathJax.ElementJax.mml;
            MML.mi.prototype.setTeXclass = function (prev) {
                this.getPrevClass(prev);
                return this;
            };
            MML.mfrac.Augment({
                setTeXclass: function (prev) {
                    this.getPrevClass(prev);
                    for (var i = 0, m = this.data.length; i < m; i++) {
                        if (this.data[i]) this.data[i].setTeXclass();
                    }
                    return this;
                }
            });
        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("SVG Jax Ready", function () {
            var FONT = MathJax.OutputJax.SVG.FONTDATA.VARIANT["-STIX-Web-variant"] || MathJax.OutputJax.SVG.FONTDATA.VARIANT["-STIX-variant"];
            delete MathJax.ElementJax.mml.mo.prototype.remapChars['°'];
            if (FONT) {
                FONT.remap[0xB0]= [0x25E6, "normal"];
                FONT.remap[0x2A]= [0x2217, "normal"];
            }

        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("MathML Jax Ready", function () {
            var PARSE = MathJax.InputJax.MathML.Parse;
            var ADD = PARSE.prototype.AddChildren;
            PARSE.Augment({
                AddChildren: function (mml, node) {
                    ADD.call(this, mml, node);
                    if (mml.type === 'mrow') {
                        var first = mml.data[0], last = mml.data[mml.data.length-1];
                        if (mml.open && !mml.data[0].Get('stretchy')) delete mml.open;
                        if (mml.close && !mml.data[mml.data.length - 1].Get('stretchy')) delete mml.close;
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("HTML-CSS Jax Ready", function () {
            var HTMLCSS = MathJax.OutputJax['HTML-CSS'];
            var DELIMITERS = HTMLCSS.FONTDATA.DELIMITERS;
            var FONT = HTMLCSS.FONTDATA.VARIANT["-STIX-variant"] || HTMLCSS.FONTDATA.VARIANT["-STIX-Web-variant"]

            var MML = MathJax.ElementJax.mml;

            MML.mrow.Augment({
              _HTMLlineBreaks: MML.mrow.prototype.HTMLlineBreaks,
              HTMLlineBreaks: function (span) {

                if (this.parent.linebreakContainer && this.Get("display") === "inline") return false;
                return this._HTMLlineBreaks(span);
              }
            });


            DELIMITERS[0x0305] = {dir: "H", alias: 0x00AF};
            DELIMITERS[0x033F] = {dir: "H", alias: 0x003D};
            DELIMITERS[0x20E1] = {dir: "H", alias: 0x2194};

            if (FONT) {
                FONT.remap[0xB0]= [0x25E6, "normal"];
                FONT.remap[0x2A]= [0x2217, "normal"];
            }

            delete MathJax.ElementJax.mml.mo.prototype.remapChars['°'];
        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("HTML-CSS multiline Ready", function () {
            var HTMLCSS = MathJax.OutputJax["HTML-CSS"];
            var MML = MathJax.ElementJax.mml;
            var PENALTY = MML.mbase.prototype.HTMLlinebreakPenalty;

            MML.msqrt.Augment({
                linebreakContainer: false,
                HTMLbetterBreak: function () {return false}
            });
            MML.mroot.Augment({
                linebreakContainer: false,
                HTMLbetterBreak: function () {return false}
            });
            MML.mfrac.Augment({
                linebreakContainer: false,
                HTMLbetterBreak: function () {return false}
            });
            MML.mspace.Augment({
                defaultDef: {
                    indentalign: MML.INDENTALIGN.AUTO,
                    indentshift: "0",
                    indenttarget: "",
                    indentalignfirst: MML.INDENTALIGN.INDENTALIGN,
                    indentshiftfirst: MML.INDENTSHIFT.INDENTSHIFT,
                    indentalignlast: MML.INDENTALIGN.INDENTALIGN,
                    indentshiftlast: MML.INDENTSHIFT.INDENTSHIFT
                },
                HTMLbetterBreak: function (info,state) {
                    if (info.values && info.values.id === this.spanID) {return false}
                    var values = this.getValues(
                        "linebreak",
                        "indentalign","indentshift",
                        "indentalignfirst","indentshiftfirst",
                        "indentalignlast","indentshiftlast"
                    );
                    var linebreakValue = values.linebreak;
                    if (!linebreakValue || this.hasDimAttr()) {
                        linebreakValue = MML.LINEBREAK.AUTO;
                    }
                    var W = info.scanW, span = this.HTMLspanElement(), w = span.bbox.w;
                    if (span.style.paddingLeft) {w += HTMLCSS.unEm(span.style.paddingLeft)}
                    if (W - info.shift === 0) {return false} // don't break at zero width
                    var offset = HTMLCSS.linebreakWidth - W;

                    if (state.n === 0 && (values.indentshiftfirst !== state.VALUES.indentshiftfirst ||
                        values.indentalignfirst !== state.VALUES.indentalignfirst)) {
                        var align = this.HTMLgetAlign(state,values),
                            shift = this.HTMLgetShift(state,values,align);
                        offset += (info.shift - shift);
                    }

                    var penalty = Math.floor(offset / HTMLCSS.linebreakWidth * 1000);
                    if (penalty < 0) {penalty = PENALTY.toobig - 3*penalty}
                    penalty += info.nest * PENALTY.nestfactor;

                    var linebreak = PENALTY[linebreakValue]||0;
                    if (linebreakValue === MML.LINEBREAK.AUTO && w >= PENALTY.spacelimit &&
                        !this.mathbackground && !this.background)
                    {linebreak = [(w+PENALTY.spaceoffset)*PENALTY.spacefactor]}
                    if (!MathJax.Object.isArray(linebreak)) {
                        if (linebreak || offset >= 0) {penalty = linebreak * info.nest}
                    } else {penalty = Math.max(1,penalty + linebreak[0] * info.nest)}

                    if (penalty >= info.penalty) {return false}
                    info.penalty = penalty; info.values = values; info.W = W; info.w = w;
                    values.lineleading = state.VALUES.lineleading;
                    values.linebreakstyle = "before"; values.id = this.spanID;
                    return true;
                }
            });


            
            PENALTY.goodbreak = [-400];

        });</script><style type="text/css">.MathJax_Hover_Frame {border-radius: .25em; -webkit-border-radius: .25em; -moz-border-radius: .25em; -khtml-border-radius: .25em; box-shadow: 0px 0px 15px #83A; -webkit-box-shadow: 0px 0px 15px #83A; -moz-box-shadow: 0px 0px 15px #83A; -khtml-box-shadow: 0px 0px 15px #83A; border: 1px solid #A6D ! important; display: inline-block; position: absolute}

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="93188ca2bdc0075e-SJC">
var dfpReady = false;
$(document).ready(function() {
    // var journalTitle = 'nano';
    var taxonomyKeywords = $('.article_header-taxonomy');
    var articleKeyword = $('meta[name="keywords"]');
    var articleTitle = $('meta[name="dc.Title"]');
    var articleDescription = $('meta[name="dc.Description"]');
    var abstractKeyword = $('p.articleBody_abstractText:contains("Keywords: ")');
    var searchTerms = [];

    if (taxonomyKeywords.length > 0) {
        $(taxonomyKeywords).children(".rlist--inline").children("li").each(function() {
            searchTerms.push($(this).text());
        });
    }
    else if (articleKeyword.length > 0) { 
        searchTerms = searchTerms.concat(articleKeyword.prop('content').split(', '));
    }
    else if (abstractKeyword.length > 0) {
        searchTerms = searchTerms.concat(abstractKeyword.text().split("Keywords: ")[1].split('; '));
    }
    else if (articleDescription.length > 0) {
        $(articleDescription).each(function() {
            articleDescriptionKeywords = $(this).prop('content');
            articleDescriptionKeywords = articleDescriptionKeywords.replace(/.,/g,"");
            articleDescriptionKeywords = articleDescriptionKeywords.replace(/\s{2,}/g," ");
            searchTerms = searchTerms.concat(articleDescriptionKeywords.split(' '));
        });
    }

    if (articleTitle.length > 0) {
        searchTerms = searchTerms.concat(articleTitle.prop('content').split(' '));
    }

    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        var mappingLeader = googletag.sizeMapping().
        addSize([750, 200], [728, 90]). 
        addSize([0, 0], [320, 50]).
        build();
        //leaderboard
        googletag.defineSlot('/8868/journal/nano/article', [728, 90], 'dfp-journal-article-leaderboard').defineSizeMapping(mappingLeader).setTargeting('location', 'leaderboard1').setTargeting('Keyword', searchTerms).addService(googletag.pubads());
        //recommend
        googletag.defineSlot("/8868/journal/nano/article", [1, 1], "dfp-journal-article-recommend").setTargeting("ntvPlacement", ["1100167"]).setTargeting("location", "recommend").setTargeting('Keyword', searchTerms).addService(googletag.pubads());
        //googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('inst',dartInstitutionType).setTargeting('memb',dartMember);
        googletag.pubads().addEventListener("slotRenderEnded", function(event) {
            console.log(event.slot.getSlotElementId() + " isEmpty: " + event.isEmpty + " | creative id: " + event.creativeId + " " + event.size[0] + "x" + event.size[1]);
            if((event.isEmpty === false) && (event.slot.getSlotElementId() != "dfp-journal-article-recommend")) {
                $("#" + event.slot.getSlotElementId()).parents(".advertisement").slideDown();
                console.log("ad display: " + event.creativeId + " " + event.size[0] + "x" + event.size[1]);
            }
            // else {
            //     console.log("no ad found");
            // }
        });
        googletag.enableServices();
        dfpReady = true;
    });
});
</script>

<script nonce="93188ca2bdc0075e-SJC">
$(function() {
    var serialCode = "ancac3";
    var books = ["reagents", "symposium", "advances", "medichemreviews", "styleguide"]
    if(books.includes(serialCode) === false) {
        // default click action
        $("[data-id]").on("mousedown", function(e) {
            var currentClickID = $(this).attr("data-id");

            if(currentClickID.includes("_hover") === false) {
                if(currentClickID.match("^article_") && !currentClickID.match("^article_abstract_CC")) {   
                    gtag('event', "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": $(this).attr("data-id") });
                }
            }
        });
        
        // Access Management icons hover
        var articleAccessManagementIconHover = false;
        var articleAccessManagementIconHoverEvent = false;
        $("[data-id='article_access_icon']").on("mouseenter", function(e) {
            if(articleAccessManagementIconHoverEvent === false) {
                articleAccessManagementIconHover = true;
                var articleAccessManagementHover =  $(this).attr("data-id") + "_hover";
                
                setTimeout(function() { 
                    if(articleAccessManagementIconHover === true) {
                        gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": articleAccessManagementHover });
    
                        articleAccessManagementIconHoverEvent = true;
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }
        });
        $("[data-id='article_access_icon']").on("mouseleave", function(e) {
            articleAccessManagementIconHover = false;
        });
    
        // articleRightsPermissionsLink hover
        var articleRightsPermissionsLinkHover = false;
        var articleRightsPermissionsLinkHoverEvent = false;
        $("[data-id='article_rights_permissions']").on("mouseenter", function(e) {
            if(articleRightsPermissionsLinkHoverEvent === false) {
                articleRightsPermissionsLinkHover = true;
                var articleRightsHover =  $(this).attr("data-id") + "_hover";
                
                setTimeout(function() { 
                    if(articleRightsPermissionsLinkHover === true) {
                        gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": articleRightsHover });
    
                        articleRightsPermissionsLinkHoverEvent = true;
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }
        });
        $("[data-id='article_rights_permissions']").on("mouseleave", function(e) {
            articleRightsPermissionsLinkHover = false;
        });
    
        // Author hover
        var articleAuthorHover = false
        var articleAuthorHoverEvent = false
        $("[data-id='article_author_info']").on("mouseenter", function(e) {
            if((articleAuthorHoverEvent === false) && ($(this).parent().hasClass("view-affs") === false)) {
                articleAuthorHover = true;
                var authorInfoHover =  $(this).attr("data-id") + "_hover";
                
                setTimeout(function() { 
                    if((articleAuthorHover === true) && (articleAuthorHoverEvent === false)) {
                        gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": authorInfoHover });
    
                        articleAuthorHoverEvent = true;
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }
        });
        $("[data-id='article_author_info']").on("mouseleave", function(e) {
            articleAuthorHover = false;
        });
    
        // CC License hover
        var articleAbstractCCHover = false
        var articleAbstractCCHoverEvent = false
        var articleDrawerCCHover = false
        var articleDrawerCCHoverEvent = false
        $(".article__cc-license__inter a").on("mouseenter", function(e) {
            if($(this).attr("data-id")) {
                if(($(this).attr("data-id") === "article_drawer_CC-License") && (articleDrawerCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                    articleDrawerCCHover = true;
                    
                    setTimeout(function() { 
                        if((articleDrawerCCHover === true) && (articleDrawerCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                            gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": "article_drawer_CC-License_hover" });
    
                            articleDrawerCCHoverEvent = true;
                        }
                    }, 1000);
                }
                else if(($(this).attr("data-id").match("^article_abstract_CC")) && (articleAbstractCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                    articleAbstractCCHover = true;
    
                    setTimeout(function() { 
                        if((articleAbstractCCHover === true) && (articleAbstractCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                            gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": "article_abstract_CC_hover" });
    
                            articleAbstractCCHoverEvent = true;
                        }
                    }, 1000);
                }
            }
            else if(($(this).hasClass("article__cc-license__link")) && (articleAbstractCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                articleAbstractCCHover = true;
                
                setTimeout(function() { 
                    if((articleAbstractCCHover === true) && (articleAbstractCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                        gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": "article_abstract_CC_hover" });
    
                        articleAbstractCCHoverEvent = true;
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }
        });
        $(".article__cc-license__inter a").on("mouseleave", function(e) {
            if(articleAbstractCCHover === true) {
                articleAbstractCCHover = false;
            }
            if(articleDrawerCCHover = true) {
                articleDrawerCCHover = false;
            }
        });
        
        // show recommeneded click delay
        var intervalCount = 0;
        var showRecommendedInterval = setInterval(function() {
            intervalCount += 100;
            if($(".show-recommended__wrapper .show-recommended").length > 0) {
                clearInterval(showRecommendedInterval);
                $("[data-id='article_drawer_RecommendedShowMore']").on("mousedown", function(e) {
                    gtag('event', "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": $(this).attr("data-id") });
                });
                $("[data-id='article_drawer_RecommendedShowLess']").on("mousedown", function(e) {
                    gtag('event', "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "High-Voltage Potassium Hexacyanoferrate Cathode via High-Entropy and Potassium Incorporation for Stable Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsnano.3c02323", "Article_Element": $(this).attr("data-id") });
                });
            }
        }, 100);
    }
});
</script>

data-db-target-of="aboutArticleMetrics" id="about-article-metrics" class="dropBlock__holder"><button class="articleMetrics_close"> <i aria-hidden="true" class="icon-close_thin"></i><span class="sr-only">close</span></button><p>Article Views are the COUNTER-compliant sum of full text article downloads since November 2008 (both PDF and HTML) across all institutions and individuals. These metrics are regularly updated to reflect usage leading up to the last few days.</p><p>Citations are the number of other articles citing this article, calculated by Crossref and updated daily.<a href="https://www.crossref.org/services/cited-by/"> Find more information about Crossref citation counts.</a></p><p>The Altmetric Attention Score is a quantitative measure of the attention that a research article has received online. Find more information on<a href="https://help.altmetric.com/support/solutions/articles/6000233311-how-is-the-altmetric-attention-score-calculated"> the Altmetric Attention Score and how the score is calculated.</a></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="article_abstract"><div class="article_abstract-title" id="Abstract" tabindex="0"><h2>Abstract</h2><div class="article__copy"><button class="article__copy__btn"><i class="article__copy__icon icon-copy-solid" aria-hidden="true"></i></button><span class="article__copy__text">Click to copy section link</span><span class="article__copy__success">Section link copied!</span></div></div><div class="article_abstract-content hlFld-Abstract" id="abstractBox" property="description"><figure id="_i1" data-index="0" class="article__inlineFigure article_abstract-img"><button class="figure-viewer__trigger" aria-label="open figure viewer"><img class="inline-fig internalNav" src="/cms/10.1021/acsnano.3c02323/asset/images/medium/nn3c02323_0007.gif" alt="" id="tgr1" property="image" style="width:405px; height:275px"></button><div class="figure-bottom-links"><div class="download-hi-res-img"><a title="High Resolution Image" href="/cms/10.1021/acsnano.3c02323/asset/images/large/nn3c02323_0007.jpeg"><span>High Resolution Image</span></a></div><div class="download-ppt"><a title="Download MS PowerPoint Slide" href="/action/downloadFigures?doi=10.1021/acsnano.3c02323&amp;id=_i1"><span>Download MS PowerPoint Slide</span></a></div></div></figure><p class="articleBody_abstractText">Prussian blue analogues (PBAs) used as sodium ion battery (SIB) cathodes are usually the focus of attention due to their three-dimensional open frame and high theoretical capacity. Nonetheless, the disadvantages of a low working voltage and inferior structural stability of PBAs prevent their further applications. Herein, we propose constructing the K<sub><i>x</i></sub>(MnFeCoNiCu)[Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub>] (HE-K-PBA) cathode by high-entropy and potassium incorporation strategy to simultaneously realize high working voltage and cycling stability. The reaction mechanism of metal cations in HE-K-PBA are revealed by synchrotron radiation X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS), <i>ex situ</i> X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (XPS), and <i>in situ</i> Raman spectra. We also investigate the entropy stabilization mechanism via  finite element simulation, demonstrating that HE-K-PBA with small von Mises stress and weak structure strain can significantly mitigate the structural distortion. Benefit from the stable structure and everlasting K<sup>+</sup> (de)intercalation, the HE-K-PBA delivers high output voltage (3.46 V), good reversible capacity (120.5 mAh g<sup>–1</sup> at 0.01 A g<sup>–1</sup>), and capacity retention of 90.4% after 1700 cycles at 1.0 A g<sup>–1</sup>. Moreover, the assembled full cell and all-solid-state batteries with a stable median voltage of 3.29 V over 3000 cycles further demonstrate the application prospects of the HE-K-PBA cathode.</p></div><div class="article__cc-license"><div class="article__cc-license__body"><p class="article__cc-license__para">This publication is licensed under the terms of your
                            institutional subscription.
                            <a href="/servlet/linkout?type=rightslink&amp;url=startPage%3D20949%26pageCount%3D13%26copyright%3DAmerican%2BChemical%2BSociety%26author%3DJunyi%2BDai%252C%2BSha%2BTan%252C%2BLifeng%2BWang%252C%2Bet%2Bal%26orderBeanReset%3Dtrue%26imprint%3DAmerican%2BChemical%2BSociety%26volumeNum%3D17%26issueNum%3D21%26contentID%3Dacsnano.3c02323%26title%3DHigh-Voltage%2BPotassium%2BHexacyanoferrate%2BCathode%2Bvia%2BHigh-Entropy%2Band%2BPotassium%2BIncorporation%2Bfor%2BStable%2BSodium-Ion%2BBatteries%26numPages%3D13%26pa%3D%26issn%3D1936-0851%26publisherName%3Dacs%26publication%3Dancac3%26rpt%3Dn%26endPage%3D20961%26publicationDate%3DNovember%2B2023" class="link--bold">Request reuse permissions.</a></p></div></div><span class="hidden" property="publisher">ACS Publications</span><div class="article_header-article-copyright">Copyright © 2023 American Chemical Society</div><div class="article_header-footer-right"><div class="articleHeaderDropzone7" data-pb-dropzone="articleHeaderDropzone7"><!-- Empty dropzone --></div><div class="article__tags article__tags--subjects"><div class="article__tags__container"><header class="article__tags__header"><h3 class="article__tags__heading">Subjects</h3><div tabindex="0" class="article__tags__tooltip"><div aria-describedby="tooltip-subjects" class="article__tags__icon"><i class="icon-info-circle-outline"></i><span class="sr-only">what are subjects</span></div><p id="tooltip-subjects" role="tooltip" class="article__tags__diff">
